modelConfigSvc.Get()\n   299→\tif err != nil {\n   300→\t\th.logger.Error(\"fetching current LLM model configuration\", log.Error(err))\n   301→\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   302→\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusInternalServerError,\n   303→\t\t\tErr:    errors.New(\"internal error loading model configuration\"),\n   304→\t\t}\n   305→\t}\n   306→\n   307→\t// Load the Provider and Model configuration data. This is surprisingly tricky, because of\n   308→\t// various contextual defaults and/or checking the user has access to the model, etc.\n   309→\tproviderConfig, modelConfig, err := resolveRequestedModel(ctx, h.logger, currentModelConfig, h.feature, request, h.getModel)\n   310→\tif err != nil {\n   311→\t\t// NOTE: We return the raw error to the user assuming that it contains relevant\n   312→\t\t// user-facing diagnostic information, and doesn't leak any internal details.\n   313→\t\th.logger.Error(\"error resolving model\", log.Error(err))\n   314→\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   315→\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusBadRequest,\n   316→\t\t\tErr:    err,\n   317→\t\t}\n   318→\t}\n   319→\n   320→\t// ensure that all features of the request (i.e. vision, tool use, etc.) are\n   321→\t// supported by the requested model\n   322→\tif err := validateRequestCapabilities(request, params, modelConfig, h.logger, h.feature, h.scope); err != nil {\n   323→\t\treturn err\n   324→\t}\n   325→\n   326→\tctx, done := Trace(ctx, string(h.scope), modelConfig.ModelName, request.MaxTokensToSample).\n   327→\t\tWithErrorP(&err).\n   328→\t\tBuild()\n   329→\tdefer done()\n   330→\n   331→\tmodelConfigInfo := types.ModelConfigInfo{\n   332→\t\tProvider: *providerConfig, // shallow copy\n   333→\t\tModel:    *modelConfig,    // shallow copy\n   334→\t}\n   335→\n   336→\t// Finally! With all the necessary information we can now create the CompletionsClient for\n   337→\t// contacting the LLM and responding to the request.\n   338→\t// Combine base scope with ScopeComponent (e.g., \"chat.deepsearch\" + \"finder\" = \"chat.deepsearch.finder\")\n   339→\tfinalScope := string(h.scope)\n   340→\tif params.ScopeComponent != \"\" {\n   341→\t\tfinalScope = finalScope + \".\" + params.ScopeComponent\n   342→\t}\n   343→\tcompletionClient, err := client.Get(\n   344→\t\tctx,\n   345→\t\th.logger,\n   346→\t\tfinalScope,\n   347→\t\tmodelConfigInfo,\n   348→\t)\n   349→\tl := trace.Logger(ctx, h.logger)\n   350→\tif err != nil {\n   351→\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   352→\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusInternalServerError,\n   353→\t\t\tErr:    err,\n   354→\t\t}\n   355→\t}\n   356→\n   357→\t// Check rate limit.\n   358→\terr = h.rl.TryAcquire(ctx)\n   359→\tif err != nil {\n   360→\t\tif unwrap, ok := err.(types.RateLimitExceededError); ok {\n   361→\t\t\treturn &unwrap\n   362→\t\t}\n   363→\t\tl.Warn(\"Rate limit error\", log.Error(err))\n   364→\n   365→\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   366→\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusInternalServerError,\n   367→\t\t\tErr:    errors.New(\"Internal server error\"),\n   368→\t\t}\n   369→\t}\n   370→\n   371→\t// Assemble the full completion request.\n   372→\tfullCompletionRequest := h.getFullCompletionRequest(request, params, modelConfigInfo, currentModelConfig.SystemPreInstruction)\n   373→\n   374→\t// Check for cody_debug command\n   375→\tdebugResult := checkForDebugCommand(*fullCompletionRequest)\n   376→\tif debugResult.IsDebugCommand {\n   377→\t\t// Only allow site admins to use debug features\n   378→\t\t// For non-admins, just ignore the debug command silently and continue with normal processing\n   379→\t\tif err := sgauth.CheckCurrentUserIsSiteAdmin(ctx, h.db); err != nil {\n   380→\t\t\th.logger.Debug(\"non-admin user used debug command, ignoring silently\", log.Error(err))\n   381→\t\t\t// Fall through to normal processing below\n   382→\t\t} else {\n   383→\t\t\t// User is admin, process the debug command\n   384→\n   385→\t\t\t// If there's an error in the debug command syntax, return it to the user\n   386→\t\t\tif debugResult.ErrorMessage != \"\" {\n   387→\t\t\t\th.logger.Info(\"Debug command syntax error\", log.String(\"error\", debugResult.ErrorMessage))\n   388→\n   389→\t\t\t\t// Use the normal streaming response infrastructure to send the error\n   390→\t\t\t\tif request.IsStream(h.feature) {\n   391→\t\t\t\t\treturn serveStreamingResponse(\n   392→\t\t\t\t\t\tsink, ctx, h.logger,\n   393→\t\t\t\t\t\t*fullCompletionRequest, &errorCompletionClient{errorMessage: debugResult.ErrorMessage},\n   394→\t\t\t\t\t\th.grAttributionTest, h.auditLog, handlerStart)\n   395→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   396→\t\t\t\t\tserveSyncResponse(\n   397→\t\t\t\t\t\tsink, ctx, h.logger,\n   398→\t\t\t\t\t\t*fullCompletionRequest, &errorCompletionClient{errorMessage: debugResult.ErrorMessage},\n   399→\t\t\t\t\t\th.auditLog, handlerStart)\n   400→\t\t\t\t}\n   401→\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   402→\t\t\t}\n   403→\n   404→\t\t\t// Run the latency test\n   405→\t\t\tif request.IsStream(h.feature) {\n   406→\t\t\t\treturn serveStreamingResponse(\n   407→\t\t\t\t\tsink, ctx, h.logger,\n   408→\t\t\t\t\tdebugResult.ModifiedRequest, &latencyTestClient{\n   409→\t\t\t\t\t\toriginalClient: completionClient,\n   410→\t\t\t\t\t\ttestCount:      debugResult.LatencyTest,\n   411→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger:         h.logger,\n   412→\t\t\t\t\t}, h.grAttributionTest, h.auditLog, handlerStart)\n   413→\t\t\t} else {\n   414→\t\t\t\tserveSyncResponse(\n   415→\t\t\t\t\tsink, ctx, h.logger,\n   416→\t\t\t\t\tdebugResult.ModifiedRequest, &latencyTestClient{\n   417→\t\t\t\t\t\toriginalClient: completionClient,\n   418→\t\t\t\t\t\ttestCount:      debugResult.LatencyTest,\n   419→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger:         h.logger,\n   420→\t\t\t\t\t}, h.auditLog, handlerStart)\n   421→\t\t\t}\n   422→\t\t\treturn nil\n   423→\t\t}\n   424→\t}\n   425→\n   426→\tif request.IsStream(h.feature) {\n   427→\t\treturn serveStreamingResponse(\n   428→\t\t\tsink, ctx, h.logger,\n   429→\t\t\t*fullCompletionRequest, completionClient, h.grAttributionTest, h.auditLog, handlerStart)\n   430→\t}\n   431→\tserveSyncResponse(\n   432→\t\tsink, ctx, h.logger,\n   433→\t\t*fullCompletionRequest, completionClient, h.auditLog, handlerStart)\n   434→\n   435→\treturn nil\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→func (h *CompletionsHandler) getFullCompletionRequest(request types.CodyCompletionRequestParameters, params types.InternalCompletionParams, modelConfigInfo types.ModelConfigInfo, systemPreInstruction string) *types.CompletionRequest {\n   439→\t// Assemble the full completion request.\n   440→\tfullCompletionRequest := types.CompletionRequest{\n   441→\t\tFeature:         h.feature,\n   442→\t\tModelConfigInfo: modelConfigInfo,\n   443→\t\tParameters:      request.CompletionRequestParameters,\n   444→\t\tVersion:         params.Client.Version,\n   445→\t}\n   446→\n   447→\t// When a global pre-chat instruction has been specified, add it as a sytem message\n   448→\t// to the beginning of the completion request.\n   449→\tif systemPreInstruction != \"\" {\n   450→\t\tfullCompletionRequest.Parameters.PrependSystemMessage(systemPreInstruction)\n   451→\t}\n   452→\n   453→\treturn &fullCompletionRequest\n   454→}\n   455→\n   456→// validateRequestModel validates that the capabilities requested in the completion params are available in the requested model\n   457→func validateRequestCapabilities(request types.CodyCompletionRequestParameters, params types.InternalCompletionParams, modelConfig *modelconfigtypes.Model, logger log.Logger, feature types.CompletionsFeature, scope Scope) error {\n   458→\t{\n   459→\t\t// Validate the vision capability\n   460→\t\tvisionCapabilityUsed := usesVisionCapability(request)\n   461→\t\t// NOTE: dotcom models have no capabilities due to CODY-3800, so\n   462→\t\t// we're going to reject all vision requests on dotcom until that\n   463→\t\t// issue is resolved.\n   464→\t\tif visionCapabilityUsed && !hasCapability(*modelConfig, modelconfigtypes.ModelCapabilityVision) {\n   465→\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"model does not support the vision capability\", log.String(\"model\", string(modelConfig.ModelRef)))\n   466→\t\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   467→\t\t\t\tErr:    errors.Newf(\"model %s does not support the vision capability. To fix this problem, remove the message content of type image_url or change the requested model.\", modelConfig.ModelRef),\n   468→\t\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusBadRequest,\n   469→\t\t\t}\n   470→\t\t}\n   471→\n   472→\t\tif visionCapabilityUsed && !visionEnabled(scope) {\n   473→\t\t\tlogger.Warn(\"vision capability is not enabled for this instance\", log.String(\"model\", string(modelConfig.ModelRef)))\n   474→\t\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   475→\t\t\t\tErr:    errors.New(\"vision capability is not enabled for this instance. To fix this problem, enable configFeatures.chatVision the site config.\"),\n   476→\t\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusBadRequest,\n   477→\t\t\t}\n   478→\t\t}\n   479→\n   480→\t\tif visionCapabilityUsed && feature != types.CompletionsFeatureChat {\n   481→\t\t\tlogger.Warn(\"vision capability is not supported for non-chat completions\", log.String(\"model\", string(modelConfig.ModelRef)))\n   482→\t\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   483→\t\t\t\tErr:    errors.New(\"vision capability is not supported for non-chat completions\"),\n   484→\t\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusBadRequest,\n   485→\t\t\t}\n   486→\t\t}\n   487→\t}\n   488→\n   489→\t{\n   490→\t\tif len(request.Tools) > 0 && !params.Client.Version.SupportsTools() {\n   491→\t\t\tlogger.Warn(\"the requested model does not support tools\", log.String(\"model\", string(modelConfig.ModelRef)))\n   492→\t\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   493→\t\t\t\tErr:    errors.Newf(\"the api-version %d does not support tools. To fix this problem, set the HTTP query parameter to api-version=%d or higher.\", params.Client.Version, types.CompletionsV6),\n   494→\t\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusBadRequest,\n   495→\t\t\t}\n   496→\t\t}\n   497→\n   498→\t\tusesToolsCapability := len(request.Tools) > 0\n   499→\t\tif usesToolsCapability && !hasCapability(*modelConfig, modelconfigtypes.ModelCapabilityTools) {\n   500→\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"model does not support the tools capability\", log.String(\"model\", string(modelConfig.ModelRef)))\n   501→\t\t\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{\n   502→\t\t\t\tErr:    errors.Newf(\"model %s does not support the tools capability. To fix this problem, remove the use of tools, change the requested model or update the model configuration to include the tools capability.\", modelConfig.ModelRef),\n   503→\t\t\t\tStatus: http.StatusBadRequest,\n   504→\t\t\t}\n   505→\t\t}\n   506→\t}\n   507→\n   508→\treturn nil\n   509→}\n   510→\n   511→func hasCapability(model modelconfigtypes.Model, capability modelconfigtypes.ModelCapability) bool {\n   512→\treturn slices.Contains(model.Capabilities, capability)\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→func usesVisionCapability(params types.CodyCompletionRequestParameters) bool {\n   516→\tfor _, message := range params.Messages {\n   517→\t\tfor _, part := range message.Content.Parts {\n   518→\t\t\tif part.Type == \"image_url\" {\n   519→\t\t\t\treturn true\n   520→\t\t\t}\n   521→\t\t}\n   522→\t}\n   523→\treturn false\n   524→}\n   525→\n   526→func respondRateLimited(w http.ResponseWriter, err types.RateLimitExceededError) {\n   527→\t// Rate limit exceeded, write well known headers and return correct status code.\n   528→\tw.Header().Set(\"x-ratelimit-limit\", strconv.Itoa(err.Limit))\n   529→\tw.Header().Set(\"x-ratelimit-remaining\", strconv.Itoa(max(err.Limit-err.Used, 0)))\n   530→\tw.Header().Set(\"retry-after\", err.RetryAfter.Format(time.RFC1123))\n   531→\n   532→\terrcode.RespondWithJSONError(w, err, \"rate_limit_exceeded\", http.StatusTooManyRequests)\n   533→}\n   534→\n   535→type errorReporters struct {\n   536→\tstreaming   func(err error)\n   537→\tattribution func(err error)\n   538→}\n   539→\n   540→func newErrorReporters(ctx context.Context, logger log.Logger, stream types.CompletionsStreamSink) errorReporters {\n   541→\treport := func(err error, kind, feature string) {\n   542→\t\tl := trace.Logger(ctx, logger)\n   543→\t\tif writeErr := stream.ReportError(err, kind); writeErr != nil {\n   544→\t\t\tl.Error(fmt.Sprintf(\"error reporting %s error\", feature), log.Error(writeErr))\n   545→\t\t}\n   546→\t}\n   547→\treturn errorReporters{\n   548→\t\tstreaming:   func(err error) { report(err, \"error\", \"streaming completion\") },\n   549→\t\tattribution: func(err error) { report(err, \"attribution-error\", \"attribution\") },\n   550→\t}\n   551→}\n   552→\n   553→// serveStreamingResponse handles streaming requests to an LLM provider,\n   554→// It writes events to an SSE stream as they come in.\n   555→func serveStreamingResponse(\n   556→\tsink types.CompletionsSink,\n   557→\tctx context.Context, logger log.Logger,\n   558→\tcompRequest types.CompletionRequest, cc types.CompletionsClient,\n   559→\ttest guardrails.AttributionTest, auditLog codyauditlog.Service,\n   560→\thandlerStart time.Time,\n   561→) error {\n   562→\tstreamer := sink.NewStreamSink()\n   563→\tif streamer == nil {\n   564→\t\treturn nil\n   565→\t}\n   566→\tdeferred := streamer.Deferred()\n   567→\tif deferred != nil {\n   568→\t\tdefer deferred()\n   569→\t}\n   570→\n   571→\terrorReporters := newErrorReporters(ctx, logger, streamer)\n   572→\n   573→\tf := guardrails.NoopCompletionsFilter(streamer.Handle)\n   574→\tif cf := conf.GetConfigFeatures(conf.SiteConfig()); cf != nil && cf.Attribution &&\n   575→\t\tfeatureflag.FromContext(ctx).GetBoolOr(\"autocomplete-attribution\", true) {\n   576→\t\tfactory := guardrails.NewCompletionsFilter\n   577→\t\t// TODO(#61828) - Validate & cleanup:\n   578→\t\t// 1.  If experiments are successful on S2 and we do not see any panics,\n   579→\t\t//     please switch the feature flag default value to true.\n   580→\t\t// 2.  Afterwards cleanup the implementation and only use V2 completion filter.\n   581→\t\t//     Remove v1 implementation completely.\n   582→\t\tif featureflag.FromContext(ctx).GetBoolOr(\"autocomplete-attribution-v2\", false) {\n   583→\t\t\tfactory = guardrails.NewCompletionsFilter2\n   584→\t\t}\n   585→\t\tff, err := factory(guardrails.CompletionsFilterConfig{\n   586→\t\t\tSink:             streamer.Handle,\n   587→\t\t\tTest:             test,\n   588→\t\t\tAttributionError: errorReporters.attribution,\n   589→\t\t})\n   590→\t\tif err != nil {\n   591→\t\t\terrorReporters.attribution(err)\n   592→\t\t} else {\n   593→\t\t\tf = ff\n   594→\t\t}\n   595→\t}\n   596→\n   597→\tdeltaText := []string{}\n   598→\tresponse := &types.CompletionResponse{}\n   599→\n   600→\t// Track approximate start time of upstream LLM request. This timestamp is captured right before\n   601→\t// calling cc.Stream(), so it's very close to when the actual upstream request begins.\n   602→\tupstreamReqStart := time.Now()\n   603→\tvar onlyOnFirstEvent sync.Once\n   604→\t// Build and send the completions request.\n   605→\tsendEventFn := func(event types.CompletionResponse) error {\n   606→\t\t// Some of the LLM backends send empty chunks that we skip forwarding to\n   607→\t\t// the client.  It's more reliable to do this check once here instead of\n   608→\t\t// having every LLM backend do this validation, which is easy to forget.\n   609→\t\t// The chat client crashes with the  error below when the `completion`\n   610→\t\t// property is missing:\n   611→\t\t//     \"Request Failed: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'length')\"\n   612→\t\tif event.IsEmpty() {\n   613→\t\t\treturn nil\n   614→\t\t}\n   615→\t\tif auditLog != nil {\n   616→\t\t\tdeltaText = append(deltaText, event.DeltaText)\n   617→\t\t\tif len(event.Completion) > 0 {\n   618→\t\t\t\tresponse.Completion = event.Completion\n   619→\t\t\t} else if len(event.DeltaText) > 0 {\n   620→\t\t\t\tdeltaText = append(deltaText, event.DeltaText)\n   621→\t\t\t}\n   622→\t\t\tif event.Model != nil {\n   623→\t\t\t\tresponse.Model = event.Model\n   624→\t\t\t\t// Record in the response what \"modelref\" (Sourcegraph canonical\n   625→\t\t\t\t// representation) was used in this request. This is required to\n   626→\t\t\t\t// correctly estimate the cost of the completion.\n   627→\t\t\t\tif event.ModelRef == nil {\n   628→\t\t\t\t\tresponse.ModelRef = new(string(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef))\n   629→\t\t\t\t}\n   630→\t\t\t}\n   631→\t\t\tif event.Usage != nil {\n   632→\t\t\t\tresponse.Usage = event.Usage\n   633→\t\t\t}\n   634→\t\t}\n   635→\t\tonlyOnFirstEvent.Do(func() {\n   636→\t\t\ttimeToFirstEventMetrics.Observe(\n   637→\t\t\t\ttime.Since(upstreamReqStart).Seconds(),\n   638→\t\t\t\t1,\n   639→\t\t\t\tnil,\n   640→\t\t\t\tstring(compRequest.Feature),\n   641→\t\t\t\tstring(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef.ProviderID()),\n   642→\t\t\t\tstring(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef.ModelID()),\n   643→\t\t\t)\n   644→\t\t})\n   645→\n   646→\t\treturn f.Send(ctx, event)\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\t// Record the time taken for initial request processing overhead before sending to the LLM provider.\n   650→\tcompletionsHandlerOverheadMetrics.Observe(\n   651→\t\ttime.Since(handlerStart).Seconds(),\n   652→\t\t1,\n   653→\t\tnil,\n   654→\t\tstring(compRequest.Feature),\n   655→\t\tstring(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef.ProviderID()),\n   656→\t\tstring(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef.ModelID()),\n   657→\t)\n   658→\n   659→\terr := cc.Stream(ctx, logger, compRequest, sendEventFn)\n   660→\tif err != nil {\n   661→\t\tl := trace.Logger(ctx, logger)\n   662→\t\tlogFields := []log.Field{log.Error(err)}\n   663→\n   664→\t\tstreamer.FatalError(ctx, l, err)\n   665→\t\tif errNotOK, ok := types.IsErrStatusNotOK(err); ok {\n   666→\t\t\tif tc := errNotOK.SourceTraceContext; tc != nil {\n   667→\t\t\t\tlogFields = append(logFields,\n   668→\t\t\t\t\tlog.String(\"sourceTraceContext.traceID\", tc.TraceID),\n   669→\t\t\t\t\tlog.String(\"sourceTraceContext.spanID\", tc.SpanID))\n   670→\t\t\t}\n   671→\t\t}\n   672→\n   673→\t\tif errors.IsAny(err, context.Canceled, context.DeadlineExceeded) {\n   674→\t\t\tl.Warn(\"canceled while streaming completions\", logFields...)\n   675→\t\t} else {\n   676→\t\t\tl.Error(\"error while streaming completions\", logFields...)\n   677→\t\t}\n   678→\n   679→\t\t// Note that we do NOT attempt to forward the status code to the\n   680→\t\t// client here, since we are using streamhttp.Writer - see\n   681→\t\t// streamhttp.NewWriter for more details. Instead, we send an error\n   682→\t\t// event, which clients should check as appropriate.\n   683→\t\terrorReporters.streaming(err)\n   684→\t\t// For internal callers, we propgate the error so it can be handled upstream\n   685→\t\treturn err\n   686→\t}\n   687→\tif f != nil { // if autocomplete-attribution enabled\n   688→\t\tif err := f.WaitDone(ctx); err != nil {\n   689→\t\t\terrorReporters.streaming(err)\n   690→\t\t}\n   691→\t}\n   692→\n   693→\tif auditLog != nil && response != nil {\n   694→\t\tif len(response.Completion) == 0 {\n   695→\t\t\tresponse.Completion = strings.Join(deltaText, \"\")\n   696→\t\t}\n   697→\n   698→\t\t// We still want to auditlog even if the user canceled the request.\n   699→\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.WithoutCancel(ctx), 10*time.Second)\n   700→\t\tdefer cancel()\n   701→\n   702→\t\taddAuditLogEntry(ctx, logger, auditLog, compRequest, *response)\n   703→\t}\n   704→\treturn nil\n   705→}\n   706→\n   707→// serveSyncResponse handles non-streaming requests to an LLM provider,\n   708→// awaiting the complete response before writing it back in a structured JSON response\n   709→// to the client.\n   710→func serveSyncResponse(\n   711→\tsink types.CompletionsSink,\n   712→\tctx context.Context, logger log.Logger,\n   713→\tcompRequest types.CompletionRequest, cc types.CompletionsClient,\n   714→\tauditLog codyauditlog.Service,\n   715→\thandlerStart time.Time,\n   716→) {\n   717→\t// Record the time taken for initial request processing overhead before sending to LLM.\n   718→\tcompletionsHandlerOverheadMetrics.Observe(\n   719→\t\ttime.Since(handlerStart).Seconds(),\n   720→\t\t1,\n   721→\t\tnil,\n   722→\t\tstring(compRequest.Feature),\n   723→\t\tstring(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef.ProviderID()),\n   724→\t\tstring(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef.ModelID()),\n   725→\t)\n   726→\tcompletion, err := cc.Complete(ctx, logger, compRequest)\n   727→\n   728→\tif err != nil {\n   729→\t\tsink.SyncResponseError(ctx, err)\n   730→\t\treturn\n   731→\t}\n   732→\n   733→\tif completion == nil {\n   734→\t\tsink.SyncResponseError(ctx, errors.New(\"no completion\"))\n   735→\t\treturn\n   736→\t}\n   737→\n   738→\tif completion.ModelRef == nil {\n   739→\t\t// Record in the response what \"modelref\" (Sourcegraph canonical\n   740→\t\t// representation) was used in this request. This is required to\n   741→\t\t// correctly estimate the cost of the completion.\n   742→\t\tcompletion.ModelRef = new(string(compRequest.ModelConfigInfo.Model.ModelRef))\n   743→\t}\n   744→\n   745→\t// On older versions of the completions API, we don't include the usage\n   746→\tif compRequest.Version < types.CompletionsV5 {\n   747→\t\tcompletion.Usage = nil\n   748→\t\tcompletion.Model = nil\n   749→\t}\n   750→\n   751→\tif compRequest.Version < types.CompletionsV6 {\n   752→\t\tcompletion.ToolCalls = nil\n   753→\t\tcompletion.DeltaToolCalls = nil\n   754→\t}\n   755→\tsink.SyncResponseSuccess(ctx, *completion)\n   756→\n   757→\tif auditLog != nil {\n   758→\t\taddAuditLogEntry(ctx, logger, auditLog, compRequest, *completion)\n   759→\t}\n   760→}\n   761→\n   762→func newCodyIgnoreCompatibilityError(reason string, statusCode int) *errcode.HTTPErr {\n   763→\tconst prefix = \"ClientCodyIgnoreCompatibilityError\"\n   764→\treturn &errcode.HTTPErr{Status: read the whole response, but without recording the time we spend parsing it in parseResponseAndUsage()\n   597→\t\tupstreamTotalLatency = time.Since(upstreamStarted)\n   598→\n   599→\t\tif upstreamStatusCode >= 200 && upstreamStatusCode < 300 {\n   600→\t\t\t// Pass reader to response transformer to capture token counts.\n   601→\t\t\tpromptUsage, completionUsage = 604→\t\t\t\tlog.Int(\"status_code\", upstreamStatusCode))\n   605→\t\t}\n   606→\t}\n   607→\n   608→\t// Apply the rate/featurelimiting middleware first, then\n   609→\t// execute our handlerFunc last.\n   610→\treturn featurelimiter.Handle(\n   611→\t\tbaseLogger,\n   612→\t\teventLogger,\n   613→\t\trs,\n   614→\t\trateLimitNotifier,\n   615→\t\thttp.HandlerFunc(handlerFunc),\n   616→\t)\n   617→}\n   618→\n   619→// Trim detected phrases to this many characters (to avoid storing too much repetitive data in BigQuery)\n   620→const phrasePrefixLength = 5\n   621→\n   622→func the\n// lifecycle of a request to an upstream API. it is not a hard-error case, and instead is a sentinel signal to\n    28→// indicate that we should try another Source.\n    29→type ErrNotFromSource struct{ Reason string }\n    30→\n    31→func (e ErrNotFromSource) Error() string {\n    32→\tif e.Reason == \"\" {\n    33→\t\treturn \"token not from source\"\n    34→\t}\n    35→\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"token not from source: %s\", e.Reason)\n    36→}\n    37→\n    38→func IsErrNotFromSource(err error) bool { return errors.As(err, &ErrNotFromSource{}) }\n    39→\n    40→// Source is the interface for actor sources.\n    41→type Source interface {\n    42→\tName() string\n    43→\t// Get retrieves an actor by an implementation-specific identifier retrieved from\n    44→\t// request headers.\n    45→\tGet(ctx context.Context, reqHeader http.Header) (*Actor, error)\n    46→}\n    47→\n    48→// ErrActorRecentlyUpdated can be used to indicate that an actor cannot be\n    49→// updated because it was already updated more recently than allowed by a\n    50→// Source implementation.\n    51→type ErrActorRecentlyUpdated struct {\n    52→\tRetryAt time.Time\n    53→}\n    54→\n    55→func (e ErrActorRecentlyUpdated) Error() string {\n    56→\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"actor was recently updated - try again in %s\",\n    57→\t\ttime.Until(e.RetryAt).Truncate(time.Second).String())\n    58→}\n    59→\n    60→func IsErrActorRecentlyUpdated(err error) bool { return errors.As(err, &ErrActorRecentlyUpdated{}) }\n    61→\n    62→type SourceUpdater interface {\n    63→\tSource\n    64→\t// Update updates the given actor's state, though the implementation may\n    65→\t// decide not to do so every time.\n    66→\t//\n    67→\t// Error can be ErrActorRecentlyUpdated if the actor was updated too recently.\n    68→\tUpdate(ctx context.Context, actor *Actor) error\n    69→}\n    70→\n    71→type SourceSyncer interface {\n    72→\tSource\n    73→\t// Sync retrieves all known actors from this source and updates its cache.\n    74→\t// All Sync implementations are called periodically - It uses a redsync.Mutex to ensure only one worker is running\n// at a time.\nfunc (s *Sources) Worker(logger log.Logger, rmux *redsync.Mutex, rootInterval time.Duration) goroutine.BackgroundRoutine {\n\tlogger = logger.Scoped(\"sources.worker\")\n\tobCtx := observation.NewContext(logger)\n\n\treturn &redisLockedBackgroundRoutine{\n\t\tlogger: logger.Scoped(\"redisLock\"),\n\t\trmux:   rmux,\n\n\t\troutine: goroutine.NewPeriodicServiceGoroutine(\n\t\t\tcontext.Background(),\n\t\t\t&sourcesSyncHandler{\n\t\t\t\tlogger:       logger.Scoped(\"handler\"),\n\t\t\t\trmux:         rmux,\n\t\t\t\tsources:      s,\n\t\t\t\tsyncInterval: rootInterval,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tgoroutine.WithName(\"sourcesSync\"),\n\t\t\tgoroutine.WithDescription(\"periodic full sources sync worker\"),\n\t\t\tgoroutine.WithInterval(rootInterval),\n\t\t\tgoroutine.WithOperation(\n\t\t\t\tobCtx.Operation(observation.Op{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:        \"sourcesSync\",\n\t\t\t\t\tDescription: \"sync actor sources\",\n\t\t\t\t})),\n\t\t),\n\t}\n}\n\n// redisLockedBackgroundRoutine attempts to acquire a redsync lock before starting,\n// and releases it when stopped.\ntype redisLockedBackgroundRoutine struct {\n\tlogger log.Logger\n\n\trmux    *redsync.Mutex\n\troutine goroutine.BackgroundRoutine\n}\n\nfunc (s *redisLockedBackgroundRoutine) Name() string {\n\treturn s.routine.Name()\n}\n\nfunc (s *redisLockedBackgroundRoutine) Start() {\n\ts.logger.Info(\"Starting background sync routine\")\n\n\t// Best-effort attempt to acquire lock immediately.\n\t// We check if we have the lock first because in tests we may manually acquire\n\t// it first to keep tests stable.\n\tif expire := s.rmux.Until(); expire.IsZero() {\n\t\tif err := s.rmux.LockContext(context.Background()); err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Attempted to claim worker lock, but failed\", log.Error(err))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Claimed worker lock\")\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Did not claim worker lock\")\n\t}\n\n\ts.routine.Start()\n}\n\nfunc (s *redisLockedBackgroundRoutine) Stop(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\ts.logger.Info(\"Stopping background sync routine\")\n\tstopErr := s.routine.Stop(ctx)\n\n\t// If we have the lock, release it and let somebody else work\n\tif expire := s.rmux.Until(); !expire.IsZero() && expire.After(time.Now()) {\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Releasing held lock\",\n\t\t\tlog.Time(\"heldLockExpiry\", expire))\n\n\t\treleaseCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 10*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tstate, err := s.rmux.UnlockContext(releaseCtx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to unlock mutex on worker shutdown\",\n\t\t\t\tlog.Bool(\"lockState\", state),\n\t\t\t\tlog.Time(\"heldLockExpiry\", expire),\n\t\t\t\tlog.Error(err))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Lock released successfully\",\n\t\t\t\tlog.Bool(\"lockState\", state))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\ts.logger.Info(\"Background sync successfully stopped\",\n\t\tlog.Duration(\"elapsed\", time.Since(start)))\n\treturn stopErr\n}\n\n// sourcesSyncHandler is a handler for NewPeriodicGoroutine\ntype sourcesSyncHandler struct {\n\tlogger  log.Logger\n\trmux    *redsync.Mutex\n\tsources *Sources\n\n\tsyncInterval time.Duration\n}\n\nvar _ goroutine.Handler = &sourcesSyncHandler{}\n\nfunc (s *sourcesSyncHandler) Handle(ctx context.Context) (err error) {\n\tvar cancel func()\n\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, s.syncInterval)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\thandleLogger := sgtrace.Logger(ctx, s.logger).\n\t\tWith(log.Duration(\"handle.timeout\", s.syncInterval))\n\n\tvar skippedReason string\n\tspan := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\t// Annotate span to indicate whether we're actually doing work today\n\t\tspan.SetAttributes(\n\t\t\tattribute.Bool(\"skipped\", skippedReason != \"\"),\n\t\t\tattribute.String(\"skipped.reason\", skippedReason))\n\t}()\n\n\tlockExpire := s.rmux.Until()\n\tswitch {\n\t// If we are not holding a lock, or the lock we held has expired, try to\n\t// acquire it\n\tcase lockExpire.IsZero() || lockExpire.Before(time.Now()):\n\t\t// If another instance is working on background syncs, we don't want to\n\t\t// do anything. We should check every time still in case the current worker\n\t\t// goes offline, we want to be ready to pick up the work.\n\t\tif err := s.rmux.LockContext(ctx); errors.HasType[*redsync.ErrTaken](err) {\n\t\t\tskippedReason = fmt.Sprintf(\"did not acquire lock, another worker is likely active: %s\", err.Error())\n\t\t\thandleLogger.Debug(skippedReason)\n\t\t\treturn nil // ignore lock contention errors\n\t\t} else if err != nil {\n\t\t\terr = errors.Wrap(err, \"failed to acquire unclaimed worker lock\")\n\t\t\tskippedReason = err.Error()\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\t// We've succesfully acquired the lock, continue!\n\t\tspan.SetAttributes(attribute.Bool(\"lock.acquired\", true))\n\n\t// If the lock has not yet expired\n\tcase lockExpire.After(time.Now()):\n\t\thandleLogger.Debug(\"Extending held lock duration\")\n\t\t// Otherwise, if the lock has not yet expired, extend our lock so that\n\t\t// we can keep working.\n\t\tif _, err = s.rmux.ExtendContext(ctx); err != nil {\n\t\t\terr = errors.Wrap(err, \"failed to extend claimed worker lock\")\n\t\t\tskippedReason = err.Error()\n\n\t\t\t// Best-effort attempt to release the lock so that we don't get\n\t\t\t// stuck. If we are here we already think we \"hold\" the lock, so\n\t\t\t// worth a shot just in case.\n\t\t\t_, _ = s.rmux.UnlockContext(ctx)\n\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\t// We've successfully extended the lock, continue!\n\t\tspan.SetAttributes(attribute.Bool(\"lock.extended\", true))\n\t}\n\n\thandleLogger.Info(\"Running sources sync\")\n\treturn s.sources.SyncAll(ctx, handleLogger)\n}\n\ntype FakeSource struct {\n\tSourceName codygatewayactor.ActorSource\n\tGetFunc    func(context.Context, http.Header) (*Actor, error)\n}\n\nfunc (m FakeSource) Name() string {\n\treturn string(m.SourceName)\n}\n\nfunc (m FakeSource) Get(_ context.Context, _ http.Header) (*Actor, error) {\n\tif m.GetFunc != nil {\n\t\treturn m.GetFunc(context.Background(), http.Header{})\n\t}\n\tpanic(\"implement me\")\n}\n\nvar _ Source = FakeSource{}\n","numLines":354,"startLine":1,"totalLines":354}}}

appropriate completion endpoint.\n\n9. **Authentication**: The auth middleware validates the incoming token through the sources, checks if access is enabled, and returns a 401 if authentication reaching the downstream LLM provider.\\n\\n## Frontend (GraphQL + HTTP API)\\n\\n**Entry points** are either the legacy GraphQL resolver (`completionsResolver.Completions` in `cmd/frontend/internal/completions/resolvers/resolver.go`) or the HTTP handlers (`CompletionsHandler.ServeHTTP` in `cmd/frontend/internal/httpapi/completions/handler.go`), registered via `NewChatCompletionsStreamHandler` / `NewCodeCompletionsHandler`.\\n\\n**Auth/enabled check #1**: `completionsapis.IsEnabled` → `cody.IsCodyEnabled` verifies Cody is licensed and active. Returns 401 if not.\\n\\n**Auth/enabled check #2**: `checkClientCodyIgnoreCompatibility` enforces a minimum client version for VS Code (>=1.20) and JetBrains (>=6.0) if CodyIgnore filters are configured. Returns 406 if the client is too old.\\n\\n**Model resolution**: `resolveRequestedModel` + `validateRequestCapabilities` checks that the requested model exists in the instance's model config and that the request's features (vision, tool use) are supported.\\n\\n**Rate limit layer #1 (Frontend / Redis)**: `rateLimiter.TryAcquire` in `limiter.go`. A per-user (or per-IP for anonymous) daily counter is stored in Redis. The limit comes from a per-user DB override (`GetChatCompletionsQuota` / `GetCodeCompletionsQuota`) or falls back to the global site config values `PerUserDailyLimit` / `PerUserCodeCompletionsDailyLimit`. Exceeding this returns `RateLimitExceededError` → HTTP 429.\\n\\n**Provider selection**: `client.Get` → `getAPIProvider` in `internal/completions/client/client.go`. Reads the model's `ServerSideConfig` to pick one of 8 backends: AWSBedrock, AzureOpenAI, OpenAICompatible, Anthropic (direct), Google, Fireworks, OpenAI (generic), or **Cody Gateway** (`SourcegraphProvider`). The selected client is wrapped in `observedClient` for metrics/tracing.\\n\\n## Cody Gateway (Proxy Service)\\n\\nIf the Sourcegraph instance is configured to use Cody Gateway (the default for sourcegraph.com and most enterprise plans), `codyGatewayClient.Stream/Complete` routes the request there.\\n\\n**Gateway Doer (`gatewayDoer`)**: Rewrites the URL to the Cody Gateway endpoint (e.g. `/v1/completions/anthropic-messages`), authenticates the request via `auther.Authenticate(req)` (attaches the Sourcegraph instance's access token), and sets headers: `X-Sourcegraph-Cody-Feature` (chat/code), `X-Sourcegraph-Scope`, interaction IDs, and the Sourcegraph actor UID.\\n\\n**Provider routing in codyGatewayClient.clientForParams**: Selects endpoint based on the model's provider ID — `anthropic` → `/v1/completions/anthropic-messages`, `fireworks`/`mistral` → `/v1/completions/fireworks`, `google` → `/v1/completions/google`, `openai` → `/v1/completions/openai`.\\n\\n**Auth layer #3 (Cody Gateway token auth)**: `Authenticator.Middleware` in `cmd/cody-gateway/internal/auth/auth.go`. Calls `Sources.Get` with request headers to resolve the actor (enterprise subscription or workspace user) from the bearer token. Returns 401 if token is unrecognized, 401 for denied credentials (logged as `EventNameUnauthorized`), or 403 if `AccessEnabled=false` (logged as `EventNameAccessDenied`).\\n\\n**Rate limit layer #2 (Cody Gateway / per-actor Redis)**: `featurelimiter.Handle` → `HandleFeature`. Calls `act.Limiter` which creates a `StaticLimiter` (with `Limit` and `Interval` per actor per feature) wrapped in `updateOnErrorLimiter`. `TryAcquire` checks the Redis counter for this actor+feature combination. Returns 429 (`RateLimitExceededError`) if exceeded, and triggers an async `Actor.Update` to refresh the actor's rate limit state from the source.\\n\\n**Upstream handler (`makeUpstreamHandler`)**: Validates the request body, runs Deep Search restriction checks, validates the model against the embedded model allowlist (`isAllowedModel`), runs abuse-detection flagging (`shouldFlagRequest`), checks model availability tracker (blocks models with recent 429s/timeouts), and finally forwards the request to the upstream LLM provider via `httpClient.Do`.\\n\\n**Upstream 429 rewrite**: If the upstream LLM provider responds with 429, it is rewritten to 503 Service Unavailable to prevent clients from directly retrying (since the rate limit window is shared across all Sourcegraph tenants). A `retry-after` header is set (default 30 seconds).\\n\\n**Downstream provider call**: For Anthropic, `NewAnthropicHandler` uses `makeUpstreamHandler` with `AnthropicHandlerMethods` which routes via Google Vertex AI (using Application Default Credentials) to the Anthropic Messages API.\\n\\n## Rate Limiting Summary\\n\\n1. **Frontend Redis daily limit** — per-user/IP, configured globally or per-user in DB, 24-hour rolling window.\\n2. **Cody Gateway actor limit** — per enterprise subscription or workspace user, per feature (chat vs code), configurable `Limit`/`Interval` per actor sourced from Enterprise Portal.\\n3. **Upstream provider 429** — rewritten to 503 at the Gateway, with retry-after to protect the shared quota.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3222,"cache_read_input_tokens":78643,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":3222,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f18bdfd3-f49c-4d91-b860-ff22e5bf448f","uuid":"474f0334-b318-4a42-91d6-e5ffe2bc6110"}

\"internal/completions/client/anthropic/anthropic.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"anthropicClient.Stream\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"summary\": \"A Cody completions request traverses multiple layers before reaching the downstream LLM provider.\\n\\n## Frontend (GraphQL + HTTP API)\\n\\n**Entry points** are either the legacy GraphQL resolver (`completionsResolver.Completions` in `cmd/frontend/internal/completions/resolvers/resolver.go`) or the HTTP handlers (`CompletionsHandler.ServeHTTP` in `cmd/frontend/internal/httpapi/completions/handler.go`), registered via `NewChatCompletionsStreamHandler` / `NewCodeCompletionsHandler`.\\n\\n**Auth/enabled check #1**: `completionsapis.IsEnabled` → `cody.IsCodyEnabled` verifies Cody is licensed and active. Returns 401 if not.\\n\\n**Auth/enabled check #2**: `checkClientCodyIgnoreCompatibility` enforces a minimum client version for VS Code (>=1.20) and JetBrains (>=6.0) if CodyIgnore filters are configured. Returns 406 if the client is too old.\\n\\n**Model resolution**: `resolveRequestedModel` + `validateRequestCapabilities` checks that the requested model exists in the instance's model config and that the request's features (vision, tool use) are supported.\\n\\n**Rate limit layer #1 (Frontend / Redis)**: `rateLimiter.TryAcquire` in `limiter.go`. A per-user (or per-IP for anonymous) daily counter is stored in Redis. The limit comes from a per-user DB override (`GetChatCompletionsQuota` / `GetCodeCompletionsQuota`) or falls back to the global site config values `PerUserDailyLimit` / `PerUserCodeCompletionsDailyLimit`. Exceeding this returns `RateLimitExceededError` → HTTP 429.\\n\\n**Provider selection**: `client.Get` → `getAPIProvider` in `internal/completions/client/client.go`. Reads the model's `ServerSideConfig` to pick one of 8 backends: AWSBedrock, AzureOpenAI, OpenAICompatible, Anthropic (direct), Google, Fireworks, OpenAI (generic), or **Cody Gateway** (`SourcegraphProvider`). The selected client is wrapped in `observedClient` for metrics/tracing.\\n\\n## Cody Gateway (Proxy Service)\\n\\nIf the Sourcegraph instance is configured to use Cody Gateway (the default for sourcegraph.com and most enterprise plans), `codyGatewayClient.Stream/Complete` routes the request there.\\n\\n**Gateway Doer (`gatewayDoer`)**: Rewrites the URL to the Cody Gateway endpoint (e.g. `/v1/completions/anthropic-messages`), authenticates the request via `auther.Authenticate(req)` (attaches the Sourcegraph instance's access token), and sets headers: `X-Sourcegraph-Cody-Feature` (chat/code), `X-Sourcegraph-Scope`, interaction IDs, and the Sourcegraph actor UID.\\n\\n**Provider routing in codyGatewayClient.clientForParams**: Selects endpoint based on the model's provider ID — `anthropic` → `/v1/completions/anthropic-messages`, `fireworks`/`mistral` → `/v1/completions/fireworks`, `google` → `/v1/completions/google`, `openai` → `/v1/completions/openai`.\\n\\n**Auth layer #3 (Cody Gateway token auth)**: `Authenticator.Middleware` in `cmd/cody-gateway/internal/auth/auth.go`. Calls `Sources.Get` with request headers to resolve the actor (enterprise subscription or workspace user) from the bearer token. Returns 401 if token is unrecognized, 401 for denied credentials (logged as `EventNameUnauthorized`), or 403 if `AccessEnabled=false` (logged as `EventNameAccessDenied`).\\n\\n**Rate limit layer #2 (Cody Gateway / per-actor Redis)**: `featurelimiter.Handle` → `HandleFeature`. Calls `act.Limiter` which creates a `StaticLimiter` (with `Limit` and `Interval` per actor per feature) wrapped in `updateOnErrorLimiter`. `TryAcquire` checks the Redis counter for this actor+feature combination. Returns 429 (`RateLimitExceededError`) if exceeded, and triggers an async `Actor.Update` to refresh the actor's rate limit state from the source.\\n\\n**Upstream handler (`makeUpstreamHandler`)**: Validates the request body, runs Deep Search restriction checks, validates the model against the embedded model allowlist (`isAllowedModel`), runs abuse-detection flagging (`shouldFlagRequest`), checks model availability tracker (blocks models with recent 429s/timeouts), and finally forwards the request to the upstream LLM provider via `httpClient.Do`.\\n\\n**Upstream 429 rewrite**: If the upstream LLM provider responds with 429, it is rewritten to 503 Service Unavailable to prevent clients from directly retrying (since the rate limit window is shared across all Sourcegraph tenants). A `retry-after` header is set (default 30 seconds).\\n\\n**Downstream provider call**: For Anthropic, `NewAnthropicHandler` uses `makeUpstreamHandler` with `AnthropicHandlerMethods` which routes via Google Vertex AI (using Application Default Credentials) to the Anthropic Messages API.\\n\\n## Rate Limiting Summary\\n\\n1. **Frontend Redis daily limit** — per-user/IP, configured globally or per-user in DB, 24-hour rolling window.\\n2. **Cody Gateway actor limit** — per enterprise subscription or workspace user, per feature (chat vs code), configurable `Limit`/`Interval` per actor sourced from Enterprise Portal.\\n3. **Upstream provider 429** — rewritten to 503 at the Gateway, with retry-after to protect the shared quota.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
